			<script type="text/javascript">
	var displayShowCaseOverlay = false;
	/**
	 * showCaseHandler
	 * Returns the current status whether the first image of the showcase has loaded
	 * @return {[type]} [description]
	 */
	var showCaseHandler = function() {
	    var isFirstImageLoaded = false;
	    var callbacks = [];

	    var getStatus = function() {
	        return isFirstImageLoaded;
	    };

	    var setStatus = function(value) {
	    	if (isFirstImageLoaded === true) {
	    		return isFirstImageLoaded;
	    	}
	        isFirstImageLoaded = true;

	        //update the status triggerCallbacks
	        setTimeout(triggerCallbacks, 5);
	        return isFirstImageLoaded;
	    };

	    var triggerCallbacks = function () {
	    	callbacks.forEach(function (callbackDetails) {
	    		if (callbackDetails.isTriggered) {
	    			return;
	    		}

	    		callbackDetails.isTriggered = true;
	    		callbackDetails.fn();
	    	});
	    };

	    var registerCallback = function (callbackDetails) {
	    	callbacks.push({
	    		key: callbackDetails.key,
	    		isTriggered: false,
	    		fn: callbackDetails.callback
	    	});
	    };

	    return {
	        getStatus: getStatus,
	        setStatus: setStatus,
	        registerCallback: registerCallback
	    };
	}();

	/*
    *	For Netflix campaign code
    */
	function fnTrackNetflixShowcaseItem (banner, state) {
		var trackers = {
			"HOC" : {
				"view" : "https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackimp/N186801.2403905BOOKMYSHOW/B9963110.134794787;dc_trk_aid=307455681;dc_trk_cid=72451480;ord=[timestamp];dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=?",
				"bannerclick" : "https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackclk/N186801.2403905BOOKMYSHOW/B9963110.134794787;dc_trk_aid=307455681;dc_trk_cid=72451480;dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=",
				"videoclick" : "https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackimp/N186801.2403905BOOKMYSHOW/B9963110.134794787;dc_trk_aid=307455681;dc_trk_cid=72451480;ord=[timestamp];dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=?"
			},
			"DD" : {
				"view" : "https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackimp/N186801.2403905BOOKMYSHOW/B9963110.134797065;dc_trk_aid=307455681;dc_trk_cid=72451480;ord=[timestamp];dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=?",
				"bannerclick" : "https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackclk/N186801.2403905BOOKMYSHOW/B9963110.134797065;dc_trk_aid=307455681;dc_trk_cid=72451480;dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=",
				"videoclick" : "https://ad.doubleclick.net/ddm/trackimp/N186801.2403905BOOKMYSHOW/B9963110.134797065;dc_trk_aid=307455681;dc_trk_cid=72451480;ord=[timestamp];dc_lat=;dc_rdid=;tag_for_child_directed_treatment=?"
			}
		};
		if (state == "view") {

			var img = new Image();
			img.src = trackers[banner]["view"];
		} else if (state == "videoclick") {

			var img = new Image();
			img.src = trackers[banner]["videoclick"];
		} else if (state == "bannerclick") {

			$("#lnkNetflixUrl").attr("href", trackers[banner]["bannerclick"]);

			window.nfCdTimerValue = 5;

			$("#spnNetflixCdTimer").html(" in " + window.nfCdTimerValue + " secs");
			BMS.Misc.modal("dBusyNetflix", true);

			window.nfCdTimer = setInterval(function () {
				if (window.nfCdTimerValue >= 1) {
					window.nfCdTimerValue--;
					$("#spnNetflixCdTimer").html(" in " + window.nfCdTimerValue + " secs");
				} else {
					clearInterval(window.nfCdTimer);
					$("#spnNetflixCdTimer").html("");
				}
			}, 1000);

			setTimeout(function () {
				window.open(trackers[banner]["bannerclick"], "_blank");
			}, 5000);
		}
	}
	function fnGoToPhysicalCardTab () {
		$('[data-type="physicalgift"]').trigger('click');
		if($('.corporate-vouchers-banner').length > 0) {
			$('html, body').animate({
	            scrollTop: $('.corporate-vouchers-banner').offset().top
	        }, 100);
		}
	}

		$('.banner-container').on('click', function() {

				obj = {},

				obj['MP:' + lotameString] = 'Click';
			}

		});

			function productClick(index){
				var clickedProduct = productClickArray[index-1];
				BMS.Misc.fnPushEventDataToAnalytics(["GA"], "", {},clickedProduct);
			}

			function csProductClickFunc(index){
				var clickedProduct = csProductClick[index-1];
				BMS.Misc.fnPushEventDataToAnalytics(["GA"], "", {},clickedProduct);
			}

			function fnChangeUrl(pathName, event) {
				try {

					$('.now-showing .__filters-clear, #touch-filter-now-showing .__filters-clear, #filter-back-button').tap();

					var myURL = window.location.pathname.substr(0, window.location.pathname.indexOf("movies"));
					window.history.pushState(null, null, myURL+"movies/"+pathName);

					if(!$('[data-filter=' + pathName + ']').find('input').is(':checked')) {
						$('[data-filter=' + pathName + ']').find('input').click();
					}
					event.preventDefault();
				} catch(e) {
					BMS.Misc.fnErr({ fnName : "fnChangeUrl", err : e });
				}
			}
		</script>

		<!-- Filter for touch-based devices -->

		<script type="text/javascript">
		$(function(){
			$('body').removeClass('_fixed');
		});

			(function(){
				/*==================================================
				=			Touch based filter section			=
				==================================================*/

				if ( global.blnIsTouchScreen ) {
					var nowShowingFilterLists = $('#touch-filter-now-showing').find('.__filter-list'),
						comingSoonFilterLists = $('#touch-filter-coming-soon').find('.__filter-list');

					toggleFilterTitle( $('#touch-filter-now-showing .__filter-title'), nowShowingFilterLists);
					toggleFilterTitle( $('#touch-filter-coming-soon .__filter-title'), comingSoonFilterLists);

					function toggleFilterTitle (filterTitle, filterLists) {
						filterTitle.on('tap', function(e) {
							var thisFilter = $(this).attr('data-filter-title');
							console.log(thisFilter);

							$(this).siblings().removeClass('_active');
							$(this).addClass('_active');

							for (var i = 0; i < filterLists.length; i++) {
								if ( $(filterLists[i]).hasClass(thisFilter) ) {
									$(filterLists[i]).addClass('_active');
								} else {
									$(filterLists[i]).removeClass('_active');
								}
							};
						});
					}

					/*=====================================================
					=			Apply filter button for touch			=
					=====================================================*/

					$('#ns-apply-button').on('tap', function () {
						$('#touch-filter-now-showing').removeClass('_active');
						$('.main-body-wrapper').css({"position": "relative"});
					});

					$('#cs-apply-button').on('tap', function () {
						$('#touch-filter-coming-soon').removeClass('_active');
						$('.main-body-wrapper').css({"position": "relative"});

					});



					/*=====  End of Apply filter button for touch  ======*/



					/*====================================================
					=			Section to Show filter button for touch			=
					====================================================*/

					$('#ns-filter-button').on('tap', function () {
						//var windowHeight = $(window).height();
						$('#touch-filter-now-showing').addClass('_active');
						//$('.__col-filters.touch').css('height', windowHeight);
						setTimeout(function () {
							$('.main-body-wrapper').css({"position": "relative"});
						}, 300);
					});

					$('#cs-filter-button').on('tap', function () {
						$('#touch-filter-coming-soon').addClass('_active');
						setTimeout(function () {
							$('.main-body-wrapper').css({"position": "relative"});
						}, 300);
					});

					/*=====  End of Section to Show filter button for touch  ======*/
				}

				/*=====  End of Touch based filter section  ======*/



				var tempCardsArray = [];
				var moviesData = $('.release-calandar aside.movie-card-container');
				//$('.release-calandar aside.movie-card-container').hide();
				//$('.release-calandar aside.movie-card-container').slice(0,8).show();
				var nsMovies = $('#now-showing .__col-now-showing .mv-row .movie-card-container');
				var movies=[];
				var cards = [];
				//nsMovies.hide();

				//Display only movies
				if(nsMovies.length==0){
					$("#now-showing .pagination .btn").hide();
				}
				// if(moviesData.length==0){
				// 	$("#now-showing .pagination .btn").hide();
				// }
				if(nsMovies.length > 8){
					nsMovies.slice(8).hide();
				}else{
					$("#now-showing .pagination .btn").hide();
				}
				//display rest of the movies
				$("#now-showing .pagination .btn").on('tap',function(events){

					$('#now-showing .__col-now-showing .mv-row .movie-card-container').slice(8).show();
					wow.scroll = true;
					wow.scrollHandler();
					$("#now-showing .pagination .btn").hide();

				});

        var currentDate = new Date();
        var currFilters = [];

        $('#now-showing .__filters-clear,#touch-filter-now-showing .__filters-clear').on('tap',function(e){
          $('#touch-filter-now-showing .filters .__checkbox input,#now-showing .filters .__checkbox input').each(function(e){
            if($(this).is(":checked")){
              $(this).trigger('click');
              $(this).trigger('tap');
            }
          });
        });

      })();
    </script>
